<TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">Re:</TD><TD>ARK ETF Trust, et al.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in"><U>File No.: 812-14172</U></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Dear Mr. Amchan:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">We are writing in
response to comments provided by the staff of the Securities and Exchange Commission (&ldquo;<U>Staff</U>&rdquo;) electronically
on March 25, 2014 with respect to an amended application (&ldquo;<U>Application</U>&rdquo;) for an order under Section 6(c) of
the Investment Company Act, as amended (&ldquo;1940 Act&rdquo;), for an exemption from Sections 2(a)(32), 5(a)(1), 22(d), and
22(e) of the 1940 Act and Rule 22c-1 under the 1940 Act, under sections 6(c) and 17(b) of the 1940 Act for an exemption from Sections
17(a)(1) and 17(a)(2) of the 1940 Act, and under Section 12(d)(1)(J) for an exemption from Sections 12(d)(1)(A) and 12(d)(1)(B)
of the 1940 Act filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission (&ldquo;<U>SEC</U>&rdquo;) on November 29, 2013, on behalf of
ARK ETF Trust, ARK Investment Management LLC and Foreside Fund Services, LLC. Below, we describe the changes made to the Application
in response to the Staff&rsquo;s comments and provide any responses to or any supplemental explanations of such comments, as requested.<FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><SUP>[1]</SUP></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><SUP>&nbsp;</SUP></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: left"><B>Comment &nbsp;1.
</B>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On page 8, in the first paragraph, please replace the third sentence with:</P>




<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.05in 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify">The Adviser to each Fund,
or its or its respective Master Fund, may enter into sub-advisory agreements with one or more affiliated or unaffiliated investment
advisers, each of which will serve as sub-advisers to a Fund, or its respective Master Fund (each, a &ldquo;Sub-Adviser&rdquo;).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.05in 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><U>Response </U>  <U>1.</U>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;We have revised the
Application accordingly.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">Comment
2.<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">On page 20, in the first
paragraph and the carryover paragraph, we note that comment 5 in our March 7<SUP>th</SUP> letter was implemented in the
incorrect place. As a result, the last three sentences of the bottom carryover paragraph (which begin, &ldquo;The
Listing Market will disseminate...&rdquo;) include an inaccurate representation and have become redundant. Therefore, please
delete these three sentences.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in"></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in"></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top"><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><SUP>[1]</SUP></FONT></TD><TD>Capitalized terms have the same meaning as in the Application unless otherwise indicated.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center; margin-bottom: 0pt">US &nbsp;&nbsp;Austin &nbsp;&nbsp;Boston &nbsp;&nbsp;Charlotte &nbsp;&nbsp;Hartford &nbsp;&nbsp;Los Angeles &nbsp;&nbsp;New York &nbsp;&nbsp;Orange
County &nbsp;&nbsp;Philadelphia &nbsp;&nbsp;Princeton &nbsp;&nbsp;San Francisco &nbsp;&nbsp;Silicon Valley</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">Comment 3.<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">On
page 28, we note the incorrect footnote was deleted. Please restore the deleted footnote (&ldquo;The Master Funds will not require

of certain PowerShares ETFs...&rdquo;).</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in"><B>Comment 4.</B><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On
page 37, in the first paragraph, in the second sentence, please delete &ldquo;or not subject to registration,.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal"><U>Response
